 Chief Minister Arvind Kejriwal has approved a scheme to compensate customers for unannounced power cuts by power distribution companies in Delhi
 dilli sarkaar ne ek bayaan main kaha ki yojana taiyaar kar uparajyapal anil baijal ko bhej di gayi he or alji kii manjuuri baad hi yah yojana prabhaav main aegi
 Under this scheme, power distribution companies will be exempted from paying penalty for the first hour of power cuts without any announcement, but for the next hour they will have to pay a fine of Rs 50 and after that a penalty of Rs 100 for every hour Will happen
 yojana ke mutabik graahakon ko diya janaa vaala muaavja unke bijli ke masik bill main joda jayega
 Apart from this, if the power distribution companies do not give compensation, then customers can also complain to the Delhi Electricity Regulatory Authority (DERC)
 yojana ke bare mendilli sarkaarne bataaya ki vidyut vitaran companiyon ko pehle ghante ke liye jurmaane main chhot din main ek baar di jaaegi
 The government hopes the Lt
 Governor will approve the policy
 aapako bataa den ki saal 2016 main kejariwal ne tatkaaleen uparajyapal najeeb jang par anirdhaarit bijli katautee ke liye graahakon ko muaavja dene se jude unki sarkaar kaa aadesh radd karne kaa aarope lagaaya tha
 Highlights of Power Reduction Compensation Scheme: - According to this new policy, in case of power cuts without prior notice, the power companies will have to ensure power supply within one hour
 agar bijli companiyaan aisa nahin kar paati hai to pehle do ghante kii katautee par 50 rupee prati ghante, prati upabhokta ko harjaana dena hoga
 In case of deduction of more than two hours, this compensation will have to be paid at Rs 100 per hour per consumer
 ek din main keval shuruaati pehle ghante kii aisi katautee kii sthiti bijli companiyon ko harjane kii chhot rahegi, lekin agar usee upabhokta ko usee din aage bhi bijli katautee kii samasya kaa saamana karnaa padataa he to companiyon ko puri katautee kaa harjaana dena padegaa
 If a consumer faces a power cut then he / she will have to complain about the power cut through SMS, e-mail, phone, app and website along with his / her name, consumer account (CA) number, mobile number etc
 bijli companiyaan ko shikaayat sweekaar kerani hogi or upabhoktaaon ko shikaayat sulajhane ke din or samay kii soochna deni hogi
 In a given time period, the consumer's CA number of damages will reach automatically and the consumer will also get information about it

" ' sienen ke anusaar, aksar al-kaayda aise pratik kaa upyog karata he

 uskaa kahana he ki usne nahin sochaa tha ki is film kaa aisa hinsak virodh hoga
 Basile said that the major problem is that he is showing on screen someone who is playing the role of Prophet Mohammad
